21:35
Erd Mun
Through the corridors of darkness, on the wings of mans desire,
Conjured by the soulless ones at the everlasting fire.
Borne on waves of insanity from mans primeval past,
The mantra of the tumult has awakened him at last.
Drawing near in the gloom comes the twilight of all shame,
The ravens of night have flown away to set Valhalla aflame.
For too long now the right hand gods have fought between themselves,
With paths that lead to paradise from this demented world.
This is the age, the age of Satan, now that the twilight is done,
Now that Satan has come.
Blue velvet shrouds the altar, black candles pierce the dark,
The skulls of the unbelievers peer sightless, bleached and stark.
The inverted cross of burnished gold the burial urns of light,
The pungent smell of incense wafts out into the night.
This is the age, the age of Satan, now that the twilight is done,
Now that Satan has come.a

Everscale News 11.05.2022 17:07:30
‚Äã‚ÄãGOSH Announcement!

Dear community,

As we all saw, the GOSH network yesterday became one of the 14 launch members of the Docker extension program at Dockercon along with some leading global IT players.¬†

GOSH is a purpose-built network leveraging the Everscale technology. It does not yet have the GOSH token. The current token called SHELL on GOSH network has a total supply of 1 trillion tokens which are provided automatically to everyone who starts using GOSH. The token is non-transferable and therefore does not have intrinsic value and cannot be traded.¬†

Currently there is a fine-tuning of GOSH tokenomics prior to its launch, but it will be beneficial to Everscale community and ecosystem due to the following: Gosh validation will be possible by Evers locked, 10 million developers will have access to Everscale technology, Docker‚Äôs endorsement of the technology will drive interest of large IT companies and there will be additional liquidity pools on Everscale with Gosh tokens.

Please join our AMA session next week to know more:
May 18th / 16:00 UTC ‚è∞

#AMA #GOSH
